\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00165}00165\ \textcolor{keyword}{def\ }test\_bootstrap\_against\_theory(method):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00166}00166\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ based\ on\ https://www.statology.org/confidence-\/intervals-\/python/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00167}00167\ \ \ \ \ rng\ =\ np.random.default\_rng(2442101192988600726)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00168}00168\ \ \ \ \ data\ =\ stats.norm.rvs(loc=5,\ scale=2,\ size=5000,\ random\_state=rng)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00169}00169\ \ \ \ \ alpha\ =\ 0.95}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00170}00170\ \ \ \ \ dist\ =\ stats.t(df=len(data)-\/1,\ loc=np.mean(data),\ scale=stats.sem(data))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00171}00171\ \ \ \ \ expected\_interval\ =\ dist.interval(confidence=alpha)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00172}00172\ \ \ \ \ expected\_se\ =\ dist.std()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00173}00173\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00174}00174\ \ \ \ \ config\ =\ dict(data=(data,),\ statistic=np.mean,\ n\_resamples=5000,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00175}00175\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ method=method,\ random\_state=rng)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00176}00176\ \ \ \ \ res\ =\ bootstrap(**config,\ confidence\_level=alpha)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00177}00177\ \ \ \ \ assert\_allclose(res.confidence\_interval,\ expected\_interval,\ rtol=5e-\/4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00178}00178\ \ \ \ \ assert\_allclose(res.standard\_error,\ expected\_se,\ atol=3e-\/4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00179}00179\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00180}00180\ \ \ \ \ config.update(dict(n\_resamples=0,\ bootstrap\_result=res))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00181}00181\ \ \ \ \ res\ =\ bootstrap(**config,\ confidence\_level=alpha,\ alternative=\textcolor{stringliteral}{'less'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00182}00182\ \ \ \ \ assert\_allclose(res.confidence\_interval.high,\ dist.ppf(alpha),\ rtol=5e-\/4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00183}00183\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00185}00185\ \ \ \ \ res\ =\ bootstrap(**config,\ confidence\_level=alpha,\ alternative=\textcolor{stringliteral}{'greater'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__resampling_8py_source_l00186}00186\ \ \ \ \ assert\_allclose(res.confidence\_interval.low,\ dist.ppf(1-\/alpha),\ rtol=5e-\/4)}
